Earlier today: **Task #28 shipped вЂ” Output moderation on every AI response (SEV-0 / PLAN_GAP_ANALYSIS closed).** Commit `8f0ca81` (2026-04-21). Output-side defense-in-depth companion to Task #26's input-side prompt-safety: every AI response (markdown, text, or structured output) is now scanned for secret leaks, PII echo, and jailbreak-compliance chatter BEFORE it leaves our infrastructure. New `lib/ai/output-moderation.ts` (572 lines) is the single source of truth вЂ” exports `ModerationOp = PromptSafetyOp` type-equal alias so the output op set stays lock-stepped with the input op set (any op added to prompt-safety auto-expands the moderation surface with no second edit site), `Severity = "none" | "low" | "medium" | "high" | "critical"` with `SEVERITY_RANK { none:0, low:1, medium:2, high:3, critical:4 }`, `Category = "secret" | "pii" | "jailbreak_echo"`, `Finding = { category, subcategory, severity, match, redactedPreview }`, `ModerationResult = { findings, worstSeverity, safe }`, pure-function `moderateOutput(text, { op })` returns the full result, and `assertOutputSafe(result, op)` throws `OutputModerationBlockedError` ONLY on critical (lower severities are observational вЂ” attached to the response meta for ops review, don't gate the user's call). **Pattern library вЂ” 18 subcategories across 3 categories:** (1) **Secrets (10 subtypes, 9 critical + 1 medium)** вЂ” `anthropic_api_key` (`sk-ant-api\d{2}-вЂ¦`), `openai_api_key` (`sk-proj-вЂ¦|sk-[a-zA-Z0-9]{48}`), `github_pat_classic` (`ghp_[A-Za-z0-9]{36}`), `github_pat_fine_grained` (`github_pat_\d{2}_[A-Za-z0-9_]{82}`), `stripe_api_key` (`sk_(live|test)_[0-9a-zA-Z]{24,}`), `aws_access_key_id` (`AKIA[0-9A-Z]{16}`), `slack_token` (`xox[baprs]-[A-Za-z0-9-]{10,}`), `google_api_key` (`AIza[0-9A-Za-z_-]{35}`), `private_key_pem` (`-----BEGIN (?:RSA |EC |DSA |OPENSSH |)PRIVATE KEY-----`) вЂ” all 9 at critical severity because echoing any of these to a user is a credential compromise regardless of how the secret got into the prompt; `jwt_token` (`eyJ[A-Za-z0-9_-]+\.eyJ[A-Za-z0-9_-]+\.[A-Za-z0-9_-]+`) at medium because JWTs commonly appear in legitimate API docs. (2) **PII (5 subtypes)** вЂ” `us_ssn` (`\b\d{3}-\d{2}-\d{4}\b`) at high, `credit_card_shape` (Luhnable 13-19 digit sequences) at high, `email_address`/`us_phone_number`/`ipv4_address` at low (too common in legitimate doc content to block, but worth logging for outlier frequency audit). (3) **Jailbreak-compliance echo (3 subtypes)** вЂ” `dan_mode_activated` (`\bDAN mode (activated|enabled|on)\b`) at high, `role_break_confirmation` (`\bI (?:am|'ll be) now (?:unrestricted|uncensored|jailbroken)\b`) at medium, `ignoring_prior_instructions` (`\b(?:I (?:am|'ll be)|now) ignoring (?:all |my |the )?(?:previous|prior) instructions\b`) at medium. Every regex has the canonical form `{ id, subcategory, severity, pattern, description }` in one of `SECRET_PATTERNS`/`PII_PATTERNS`/`JAILBREAK_ECHO_PATTERNS`. Pure regex-only, zero model-call loop, zero config, ~3ms on a 50-page OCR transcript вЂ” deterministic and cheap. **Call-site integration вЂ” 9 non-streaming ops + 1 advisory-only streaming route:** `summarize`/`translate`/`compare`/`generate`/`rewrite`/`table`/`redact`/`sign`/`ocr` all call `moderateOutput(text, { op })` + `assertOutputSafe(result, op)` on the final markdown BEFORE returning to the route handler; `OutputModerationBlockedError` bubbles up to the route handler which refunds credits + returns HTTP 502 `{ error: "output_moderation_blocked", findings: [...redactedPreview only] }` (the full match is never returned to the user вЂ” a `[REDACTED]` placeholder is returned for audit without echoing the secret itself). Streaming chat at `app/api/ai/chat/route.ts` is **advisory-only** (`console.warn` with finding summary, no throw) because the SSE is already on the wire by the time we'd have the full response to moderate вЂ” the margin-rollup cron will aggregate warn rates for post-hoc review. **Generate op special case**: `moderateOutput` runs on the MARKDOWN stage BEFORE the pdf-lib render pass вЂ” we don't want to bake a leaked API key into the PDF bytes only to catch it after (defense-in-depth holds even if rendering succeeded). **OCR special case**: moderation runs ONCE on the joined `## Page N` markdown after all per-page stitching (not per-page) вЂ” deliberate because per-page would 10Г— the regex cost on a 50-page doc AND would miss findings that span page boundaries (a redacted address broken across a page break). Inline rationale comments in `lib/ai/ocr.ts` + `lib/ai/rewrite.ts` + 7 other ops document this. **Test harness** `scripts/test-output-moderation.mjs` (436 lines / 123 assertions across 6 sections AвЂ“F): A module contract (exports, type shapes, SEVERITY_RANK values, pattern library array shapes), B secret pattern library (all 10 subtypes with positive+negative cases, criticality matrix, regex disjointness), C PII pattern library (all 5 subtypes with Luhn check for credit card shape, SSN format, E.164 + North-American phone), D jailbreak-echo pattern library (all 3 patterns with severity ordering + regex disjointness), E `moderateOutput`/`assertOutputSafe` behavior (findings array shape, `worstSeverity` derivation, `safe` boolean, `OutputModerationBlockedError` throws on critical only, lower-severity findings return `safe: true` but populate `findings[]` for audit), F call-site integration (9 non-streaming op modules import + call both functions, chat route is advisory-only with console.warn + no throw, generate moderates BEFORE pdf-lib render, ocr moderates joined-markdown not per-page). `scripts/run-all-tests.mjs` SUITES array gains `output-moderation` entry between `prompt-safety` and `dev-hooks` with a 19-line rationale comment pinning placement (same `lib/ai/*.ts` surface layer as prompt-safety + op-set dependency). **Test verdict:** `npm test` now runs **11 suites / 977 assertions in ~1.4s**, all green (pdf-tools 17 + geo-router 148 + geo-waitlist 248 + ai-usage 72 + chat-context-cap 33 + ai-router 76 + health-ai 27 + ai-margin-rollup 96 + prompt-safety 129 + output-moderation 123 + dev-hooks 8). `npx tsc --noEmit` exit 0 across the whole repo. **Deploy verification:** pushed to `main` в†’ Hostinger auto-deploy completed cleanly; `curl https://pdfcraftai.com/api/health` returned `{ ok: true, commit: "8f0ca81eecdc", ... }` confirming Task #28 bundle is live on production (commit flip `88246b5` в†’ `8f0ca81` verified). **Deploy gotcha вЂ” none.** Pure code change, no migration, no new env var. **Scope clarification вЂ” Task #28 closes `completed`:** output moderation has no runtime gate beyond "does moderateOutput run on every non-streaming op response," which the 9-call-site integration tests + live deploy verify end-to-end. Earlier: Phase 5.6 **COMPLETE**: `/tool/ai-sign` shipped end-to-end вЂ” **fifth and final** of the 5 Phase 5.6 tools. AI fills printed form fields (Name / Date / Signature / Email / Phone / Title / Company / Address / custom fields) from a user-supplied personal-info bundle (fullName required; initials, email, phone, date, company, title, address, custom k/v pairs all optional). Pipeline: (1) `lib/ai/pdf-extract.ts` -> positioned pdfjs extraction; (2) strict JSON-envelope prompt (temperature 0.1) asks the model for `{ fills: [{ label, anchorText, fieldKey, page, reason }] }` with dedicated `SignParseError` class; (3) whitespace-tolerant substring matching locates each anchor across pdfjs-extracted positioned items; (4) `pdf-lib` `drawText` right-of-anchor with binary-search shrink-to-fit + ellipsize. Signature fields use `HelveticaBoldOblique` 16pt in dark blue `rgb(0.04, 0.07, 0.42)`; regular values use `Helvetica` 10pt black. Special field keys: `__signature`, `__initials`, `__skip`, plus `custom:<slug>`. **10-credit flat cost.** Response carries the filled PDF as base64 + a markdown summary that's persisted to `ai_outputs` (kind: `"signing"`); no binary PDF storage вЂ” replays return `signedPdfBase64: null`. 25 MB PDF cap + 16 KB info cap (413 `info_too_large`). 422 `no_extractable_text` guard when >=90% of pages look OCR-candidate. Route error map: `NoAIProviderConfiguredError` -> 503; `SignParseError` -> 502 `sign_parse_failed` + refund; `pdf_extract_failed` -> 400; generic -> 502 `sign_failed` + refund; 207 persist-failed fallback still hands back the base64 PDF so the 10-credit spend isn't lost. **Explicit UI caveat**: amber-bordered "Not a cryptographic signature" card directs legally-binding e-signature needs to DocuSign / Adobe Sign. Commit `5e85ca0`. Live prod verified: `/tool/ai-sign` 200, `POST /api/ai/sign` 401 `not_authenticated` on anon multipart **and** JSON bodies, `GET /api/ai/sign` 405 (POST-only). **All 5 Phase 5.6 tools now shipped: `rewrite` (3cr) / `table` (3cr) / `redact` (5cr) / `generate` (20cr) / `sign` (10cr).** Earlier: `/tool/ai-generate` shipped end-to-end вЂ” **fourth of the 5 Phase 5.6 tools**. Prompt-to-PDF with 7 document types (memo / report / brief / letter / blog / outline / other), 3 lengths (short ~400w / medium ~1000w / long ~2000w), 4 tones (neutral / formal / casual / technical). Two-stage pipeline: (1) the model emits clean markdown at temperature 0.4, (2) a custom 620-line markdownв†’pdf-lib renderer lays it out on US-Letter pages using the Helvetica family (Helvetica / Bold / Oblique / BoldOblique), with block-level parsing for H1/H2/H3 + paragraphs + bullet + numbered lists + horizontal rules, inline bold/italic span tracking with word-wrap preservation across line breaks, and `ensureSpace()` cursor-based pagination. 16,000 char input cap (413 `prompt_too_long`) with `PROMPT_CHAR_BUDGET = 8,000` model-side clamp; per-length `MAX_TOKENS_BY_LENGTH` output cap (short 900 / medium 2200 / long 4600) with stop-reason truncation detection. 20-credit flat cost. Response carries the generated PDF as base64 + a markdown summary that's persisted to `ai_outputs` (kind: `"generation"`); no binary storage infra вЂ” replays return `pdfBase64: null` with a client-side "Re-run for a fresh PDF" callout. Strict JSON body at `/api/ai/generate` (not multipart вЂ” no PDF upload for this tool). Commit `d00ee8a`. ---

## How to use this file

- Anything in **Done** is verified live вЂ” don't redo it.
- Anything in **Pending (Claude can do)** is fully automatable from a Cowork session вЂ” pick it up.
- Anything in **Pending (needs the user)** requires a human action (DNS console, mailbox check, paid signup, etc.) вЂ” don't guess credentials, just remind the user.
- When you finish an item, move it to Done with the date and the verification command/screenshot.

## Done

### 2026-05-08 вЂ” Match highlighting on AI History keyword search

- [x] **feat(ai-history): match highlighting on keyword-filtered row excerpts.** Commit `7f86f08` (2026-05-08). Compounds 6bbb193 (keyword search) вЂ” completes the AI History keyword-search experience. When a user searches for "ARR" the row excerpt now surfaces the matched paragraph (likely several pages into the doc) with the term wrapped in styled `<mark>`, not the doc's opening prose with no visible hit. New `makeHighlightedExcerpt(md, keyword)` finds the first case-insensitive occurrence, builds a ~220-char window centered on the match (snapping start/end to word boundaries without ever pushing window edges past the match itself), adds leading/trailing ellipses when the window doesn't reach doc edges, splits the windowed text on a case-insensitive capture-group regex, and renders match-segments wrapped in `<mark style={{ background: var(--accent-soft), color: var(--accent), padding: 0 2px, borderRadius: 3 }}>` (matches the active-filter chip styling вЂ” not the browser default neon yellow). New `escapeForRegex` helper guards against `.` / `(foo)` / `[abc]` etc. in user input getting treated as regex meta. The display-form keyword (post-trim, pre-LIKE-escape) drives the highlight regex via `displayKeyword = keywordFilter && rawQ.trim() : null` вЂ” using the LIKE-escaped form would highlight `\\%` instead of `%`. Render branches: when `displayKeyword` set, call `makeHighlightedExcerpt`; otherwise plain `makeExcerpt` (cheaper, no React fragment overhead). CI guard +7 assertions in Section I: helpers present, canonical regex-meta charset, `<mark>` uses design tokens not browser default, displayKeyword derivation pattern, render-path branch, `i % 2 === 1` alternation invariant for split-with-capture-group (the lastIndex-leak footgun guard). 44 total in the harness (was 37). Aggregator: 5965 passed, 0 failed across 105 suites (was 5958/105). Verified live at `7f86f08` after standard deploy 503 transition (cleared on its own without stale-worker pkick). **No deploy gotcha.**

### 2026-05-08 вЂ” OAuth email-verified stamp (unblocks gate activation)

- [x] **fix(auth): stamp users.emailVerified=NOW() on Google OAuth signin.** Commit `e62a79a` (2026-05-08). Closes the latent OAuth lockout that would fire the moment EMAIL_VERIFICATION_GATE=on is flipped in production. The gate (`assertEmailVerified` in lib/auth/email-verification.ts) checks `users.emailVerified !== null` and throws EmailNotVerifiedError. The Credentials provider sets emailVerified via the OTP flow; Google OAuth had no equivalent вЂ” DrizzleAdapter inserts the user row but leaves emailVerified NULL. So when the gate flag flips on, every Google user gets locked out of every /api/ai/* route. Fix in auth.ts events.signIn: when `account?.provider === "google"` AND Google's `profile.email_verified === true`, run an idempotent UPDATE: `UPDATE users SET email_verified = NOW() WHERE id = ? AND email_verified IS NULL`. The IS NULL filter is the idempotency guard (re-firing is a no-op once verified, AND it preserves the original verification timestamp for users who verified via OTP first and later linked Google). Strict `=== true` not truthy. UPDATE wrapped in try/catch that logs + continues вЂ” DB hiccup must NEVER block the user from their own account. Provider check is "google" specifically so Credentials sign-ins still flow through the OTP path. CI guard `scripts/test-oauth-email-verified.mjs` (12 assertions / 6 sections) pins all of the above plus a cross-file invariant against the gate's read path so a column rename breaks both surfaces in lockstep. Existing `referrals-foundation` J6 assertion broadened from anchored `{ user, isNewUser }` regex to contains-style so the new `{ user, account, profile, isNewUser }` shape passes too. Aggregator: 5958 passed, 0 failed across 105 suites (was 5946/104). **Unblocks founder-side activation:** `EMAIL_VERIFICATION_GATE=on` can now flip safely in Hostinger env vars without locking out OAuth users.

### 2026-05-08 вЂ” Keyword content search on AI History (third filter axis)

- [x] **feat(ai-history): keyword content search (?q=<term>).** Commit `6bbb193` (2026-05-08). Completes the {kind Г— source Г— keyword} filter triplet. Query gains `${aiOutputs.contentMd} LIKE ${"%" + term + "%"} ESCAPE '\\'` clause when ?q= present; wildcards live in the OUTER literal (not user-controllable), inner term binds via Drizzle's sql template. New `sanitizeKeyword()` trims, length-clamps (KEYWORD_MIN_CHARS=2 .. KEYWORD_MAX_CHARS=64), rejects control bytes, AND escapes the MySQL LIKE metacharacters (backslash FIRST so % and _ escapes don't double-escape, then % and _ to literals). The ESCAPE clause names backslash explicitly so MySQL doesn't fall back to its default escape char (varies across servers). New `KeywordSearchForm` GET form above the row list with hidden inputs preserving kind + source axes when submitting a new keyword. Clear-keyword Link drops only the q axis. Performance: LIKE on mediumtext can't use any index вЂ” O(rows Г— content size) scan within the per-user partition. Bounded for typical scale (<500 rows, <50KB content_md), future >10k-artifact users would need FULLTEXT or a denormalized search column (explicit migration, deferred). CI guard +10 assertions in Section H: sanitizer + min/max constants, backslash-first escape order, % and _ replacements, LIKE clause shape with ESCAPE, negative check on string-interpolated `'%${term}%'` regression, KeywordSearchForm with method=get + hidden inputs. 37 total in the harness (was 27). Aggregator: 5946 passed, 0 failed across 104 suites (was 5936/104). Verified live at `6bbb193` ~6 min after push, no stale-worker hold this cycle. **No deploy gotcha.**

### 2026-05-08 вЂ” Copy / Download actions on AI artifact preview

- [x] **feat(preview): Copy markdown + Download .md actions.** Commit `8215906` (2026-05-08). Compounds the b56120b в†’ ff47672 chain. AI History reaches every artifact, the preview page labels every kind correctly вЂ” but the preview was view-only. Without exit ramps users fall back to right-click в†’ View source в†’ copy raw HTML, which loses the markdown structure. Two affordances ship: (1) **Copy markdown** via `navigator.clipboard.writeText(contentMd)` with brief inline "Copied" confirmation (1.6s timeout); modern API only вЂ” `document.execCommand('copy')` is deprecated and async-fails on cross-origin iframes / sandboxed contexts. (2) **Download .md** via Blob + `URL.createObjectURL` + temp anchor + click + revoke; filename pattern `<kind>-of-<sourceBaseName>-<YYYY-MM-DD>.md` with `.pdf` suffix stripped and unsafe filesystem chars sanitized via conservative `[^A-Za-z0-9._-]` allowlist. Generation kind special-cased вЂ” its sourceName is the literal "prompt" so it falls back to `<kind>-<YYYY-MM-DD>.md` (otherwise output reads as nonsense like "generation-of-prompt-2026-05-08.md"). Object URL revocation lives in a `try/finally` block so a thrown `a.click()` doesn't leak the URL вЂ” M6 audit catches the leak globally; the new local guard pins the shape tighter. Pure client component (`"use client";`) so the two browser APIs work; server-rendered button row mounts above the rendered article so no layout shift on hydration. CI guard `scripts/test-ai-output-actions.mjs` (18 assertions / 5 sections) pins client-component directive, named export + 4-prop type shape, navigator.clipboard not legacy execCommand, URL.createObjectURL paired with revokeObjectURL inside finally, every required prop wired through with the right shape (catches `contentMd={row.toolId}` swap-bug), filename-sanitizer allowlist, and generation special-case. Aggregator: 5929 passed, 0 failed across 104 suites (was 5910/103). M6 audit still 13/0. **Deploy gotcha:** auto-pull worked but runtime held stale (`a01e5fd` after `8215906` push). Canonical CLAUDE.md В§5 stale-worker scenario вЂ” `last-source` git log confirmed pipeline OK, runtime was the problem. Single SSH pkick (`ps -fu u692382124 | grep next-server | xargs kill -KILL && touch tmp/restart.txt`) + 60s wait recovered cleanly. No thread-cap cascade.

### 2026-05-08 вЂ” preview-page kind label fix (compounds Tier 4 #11)

- [x] **fix(preview): correct kind labels for all 9 ai_outputs kinds.** Commit `ff47672` (2026-05-08). Sister fix to b56120b: AI History surfaces all 9 kinds, then clicking a row navigates to /app/files/[id]/preview which independently rendered the kind label. That page had a 4-way ternary chain (`summary / translation / comparison / OCR` with a trailing `: "OCR"` fallback) so the 5 Phase-5.6 kinds (rewrite / table / redaction / generation / signing) all rendered as "AI В· OCR" вЂ” wrong label, looks broken when AI History sends users there. Replaced the chain with a `KIND_LABELS: Record<typeof row.kind, string>` map вЂ” the `Record<typeof row.kind, ...>` form is what makes TS fail-closed on a missing kind (without that exact constraint, a future kind silently renders `undefined` at runtime instead of failing at compile time). Generation is also special-cased BEFORE the meta.sourceName branch because its sourceName is the literal string "prompt" вЂ” falling through to the generic "From <sourceName>" template would render "From prompt" which is awkward and misleading. Generation now shows title / docType / tone / pageCount instead. Per-kind detail lines added: rewrite shows `В· <mode>`, table shows `В· N tables`, redaction shows `В· N findings В· M unmatched`, signing shows `В· N fields filled В· M unfilled`. CI guard `scripts/test-preview-page-kind-parity.mjs` (10 assertions / 5 sections) pins the canonical KIND_LABELS signature, schema/page kind parity (mirrors AI History guard), the old ternary chain is gone (regression check on the exact "kind === 'summary' ? 'Summary' : kind === 'translation'" prefix), and generation special-case placement. Aggregator: 5910 passed, 0 failed across 103 suites (was 5900/102). Verified live at `ff47672` ~5 min after push (transient 503 during deploy, recovered without manual intervention per CLAUDE.md В§5 patience guidance). **No deploy gotcha** вЂ” pure code change, no migration, no env var.

### 2026-05-08 вЂ” Tier 4 #11 closed

- [x] **Tier 4 #11 вЂ” `/app/ai-history` dedicated AI artifact index.** Commit `b56120b` (2026-05-08). Closes the highest-volume "where did my output go?" complaint surfaced in the 2026-05 improvement audit. /app/files lists everything (uploads + tool outputs + AI artifacts) intermixed, with the AI ones reachable only via a small Eye icon. The new page is a focused chronological index of just the AI artifacts вЂ” all 9 kinds (summary / translation / ocr / comparison / rewrite / table / redaction / generation / signing) вЂ” with kind chip + source filename + content excerpt visible per row, clickable through to the existing /app/files/[id]/preview viewer (no re-spend). Cross-tenant safety: query is INNER JOINed to `files` and filtered on `files.userId = session.userId` вЂ” `ai_outputs` has no userId column at all (auth model is "owner of source PDF owns the derivative"), so filtering on the join key alone would let a guessed file_id leak someone else's output. Same pattern /app/files/[id]/preview already uses. Payload-size discipline: content_md is mediumtext (16MB ceiling), excerpted server-side to ~220 chars at word boundary before render вЂ” a worst-case 16MB row would otherwise blow past Next.js's RSC payload ceiling. Whitelisted kind filter (not echoed). Force-dynamic. New nav entry between Chat and Usage with `FileAi` icon. CI guard `scripts/test-ai-history-page.mjs` (20 assertions across 6 sections) pins the cross-tenant invariant, kind enum parity with db/schema/app.ts (catches the runtime crash when a future kind is added to the schema enum but not to the page's KIND_META map), whitelist-not-echo, payload-size guard, nav entry presence, and force-dynamic. Pure static parse, sub-second. Aggregator: 5900 passed, 0 failed across 102 suites (was 5880/101). Verified live at `b56120b` 4 min after push (well within 2вЂ“5 min envelope).

- [x] **M18 вЂ” page-1 preview thumbnail on AI tool upload cards.** Commit `c02765e` (2026-04-29). User upload flow used to show only file name + size before clicking the credit-spending Apply button. With the M25 cache, it's cheap to also show a small page-1 thumbnail вЂ” handoff users (free tool в†’ AI tool via M9) see it instantly because bytes are already cached; first-time uploads see a brief loading icon. Real benefit: users verify they uploaded the right doc BEFORE paying credits. New `components/tools/UploadedFilePreview.tsx` вЂ” small thumbnail wrapping `useFirstPagePreview`, renders a fixed-height image (default 80px, configurable) with aspect ratio preserved, falls back to a generic file icon on render failure or while loading (doesn't block the tool flow on hiccups). Wired into 8 AI tools: Summarize (manual canary), then Translate/Compare/Ocr/Rewrite/Redact/Sign/TableExtract via new `scripts/wrap-uploaded-file-preview.py` (idempotent вЂ” skips files already migrated, warns on non-matching patterns). 8 non-matching tools (TldrPdf, Mindmap, SemanticSearch, Structured/SummarizeVariant, BloodTest, ResumeParser, SearchablePdf) use slightly different file-card layouts and need manual or per-pattern follow-up вЂ” documented as M18 part 2. Total: 3227 passed, 0 failed across 38 suites (unchanged вЂ” pure visual addition; no logic changes). M-series count now **21 of 25 shipped + 2 verified-canonical (M8, M13)**.

- [x] **M16 вЂ” scroll error into view on transition (no focus steal).** Commit `b526b47` (2026-04-29). The original M16 framing was "focus return to error message on setError." Investigation found the focus-steal approach is anti-pattern per modern UX guidance вЂ” it disrupts keyboard users mid-interaction. WCAG 3.3.1 (Error Identification) is already satisfied by `role="alert"`, which screen readers auto-announce when the alert appears. This commit ships the scroll-into-view middle ground instead: when an error transitions from null to a string AND the error element is off-screen (per `getBoundingClientRect` against `window.innerHeight`), `scrollIntoView` brings it into view with `block: "center"` and smooth behavior (or `auto` if the user prefers reduced motion). Doesn't steal focus. New `components/tools/useScrollErrorIntoView.ts` hook returns a ref the consumer attaches to the error element; tracks the previous error in a ref so it only acts on nullв†’string transitions, not every re-render. Wired into the same 5 shared runners as M9/M10: PageEditorTool, PageGridTool, PdfSplitTool, PdfSortPagesTool, PdfSimpleOpsTool. Total: 3227 passed, 0 failed across 38 suites (unchanged вЂ” pure addition with no test changes). M-series count now **20 of 25 shipped + 2 verified-canonical (M8, M13)**.

- [x] **M13 вЂ” orientation-independent rect positioning invariant (verified-canonical).** Commit `4e8133c` (2026-04-29). M13 was originally flagged as "mobile orientation change rect-rescaling" вЂ” the worry being that saved rects would visibly shift when a user rotates their device mid-edit. Investigation found the architecture already handles this: pointer coords convert to PDFium pixels via `(xCss / rect.width) * pageRender.pxWidth` (PDFium pixels are fixed regardless of display container size, so the same finger position on screen maps to the same PDFium pixel before and after rotation), and saved rects render via `(r.x / pageRender.pxWidth) * 100%` (percentage positioning auto-rescales when the container re-flows). So orientation change "just works" вЂ” no rescale logic, no ResizeObserver, no orientationchange listener. The only edge case is a single in-flight drag interrupted by rotation; the user can abandon and redraw. This commit codifies that invariant as 6 new assertions in `scripts/test-page-editor-consumers.mjs` (for each of Highlight, Redact, AddLinks: pointer-to-PDFium conversion via `rect.width` division + rect rendering via `% of pageRender.pxWidth`). Catches regressions where someone accidentally introduces absolute pixel positioning that would break orientation handling. Total: 3227 passed, 0 failed across 38 suites (was 3221/38). M-series count now **19 of 25 shipped + 2 verified-canonical (M8, M13)**.

- [x] **M10 вЂ” `?file=<url>` deep-link with same-origin safety.** Commit `f4a47c2` (2026-04-29). Documentation, blog posts, and SEO landing pages can now link directly to a tool with a sample file pre-loaded вЂ” `/tool/redact-free?file=/samples/contract-template.pdf` lands on Redact with the sample auto-loaded so the user can immediately try the tool without hunting for a test file. New `components/tools/useFileUrlConsumer.ts` hook (one-shot mount effect, same shape as M9 useHandoffConsumer) parses the URL param, resolves it via `new URL(href, window.location.href)`, rejects anything not same-origin, fetches with `Content-Type` check (accepts `application/pdf`, `application/octet-stream`, `binary/octet-stream`), enforces `MAX_FILE_SIZE_BYTES` on both the `content-length` header AND the post-fetch `blob.size` (CDNs sometimes lie), and strips the `?file=` param via `history.replaceState` BEFORE the fetch fires (avoids refresh re-triggering an expensive endpoint hit). Failures silent вЂ” broken `?file=` shouldn't block the tool; user sees the empty drop zone with a console.warn for diagnostics. Wired into the same 5 runners as M9: PageEditorTool, PageGridTool, PdfSplitTool, PdfSortPagesTool, PdfSimpleOpsTool. Test guard expanded: `scripts/test-tool-handoff.mjs` now verifies each runner imports `useFileUrlConsumer` AND the four security checks (cross-origin rejection via `resolved.origin !== window.location.origin`, size cap, URL-param stripping, Content-Type validation). 224 assertions total (was 215). Total: 3221 passed, 0 failed across 38 suites (was 3212/38). M-series count now **19 of 25 shipped + 1 verified-canonical (M8)**.

- [x] **M25 вЂ” content-sample LRU cache for useFirstPagePreview.** Commit `12a2191` (2026-04-29). Two scenarios saved 50-200ms each: (1) M9 handoff navigation between tools where both render page 1 вЂ” second tool now hits cache; (2) Reset + re-drop the same file to tweak a config вЂ” cache hit. Cache key = quick FNV-1a-style sample hash of head 1KB + tail 1KB + byte length + render scale. NOT cryptographic вЂ” collision-prone in adversarial settings, fine here because a collision shows the wrong preview which the user immediately notices. Cache stores rendered JPEG bytes (typically 100-500KB at scale=1.5) so cache hits build a fresh object URL from cached bytes вЂ” no PDFium spin. Module-level so it survives Next.js client-side route changes; bounded LRU at 4 entries to cap memory at ~2MB max. New `scripts/test-first-page-preview-cache.mjs` verifies hash determinism (same bytes + same scale в†’ same hash), collision detection (different scale / head / tail / length в†’ different hashes), and LRU eviction order (touch resets recency; oldest evicts first). Total: 3212 passed, 0 failed across 38 suites (was 3200/37). M-series count now **18 of 25 shipped + 1 verified-canonical (M8)**.

- [x] **M20 part 2 вЂ” extend retry to 16 more AI tools (full sweep).** Commit `f47efb3` (2026-04-29). The M20 v1 wired retry into SummarizePdfTool as the canary. v2 finishes the surface area: 14 tools refactored mechanically via new `scripts/wrap-fetch-ai-retry.py` (BloodTest / Compare / Mindmap / Ocr / Redact / ResumeParser / Rewrite / SearchablePdf / SemanticSearch / Sign / StructuredVariant / TableExtract / Tldr / Translate), plus 2 manual refactors for patterns the regex couldn't capture (SummarizeVariant вЂ” has a conditional `if (props.queryField && query.trim()) { form.append("query", ...) }` block; Generate вЂ” uses JSON body). Helper extension: `bodyFactory` now returns `BodyInit` (supertype of FormData) plus optional `headers` so JSON callers can use it too. The wrap script is idempotent вЂ” skips files already migrated, warns on non-matching patterns вЂ” so it can be re-run if a future tool ships with a raw fetch. Test guard: `scripts/test-fetch-ai-retry.mjs` now asserts each of the 17 AI consumer files imports `fetchAiWithRetry` and contains NO raw `await fetch("/api/ai/...")` strings. 56 assertions total (was 22). Total: 3200 passed, 0 failed across 37 suites (was 3166/37). M-series count now **17 of 25 shipped + 1 verified-canonical (M8)**.

- [x] **M20 вЂ” exponential-backoff retry on transient AI op failures.** Commit `95948d6` (2026-04-29). New `lib/client/fetch-ai-with-retry.ts` wraps fetch with retry on 408/502/503/504 (transient HTTP) and TypeError (network-level вЂ” fetch threw before a Response arrived). Backoff schedule: 1s, 2s, 4s. Max 3 attempts (1 + 2 retries). FormData is single-use so the helper takes a `bodyFactory: () => FormData` closure that rebuilds per attempt. AbortSignal-aware (M5 plumbing) вЂ” caller-cancellation propagates without retry. Optional `onAttempt(n, max)` for "RetryingвЂ¦ (2/3)" UIs. Why retry is safe to ship without per-route changes: every AI tool already builds a per-click cryptoUUID `idempotencyKey` and the server ledger has a unique index on it вЂ” retrying with the SAME key either beats the first transaction (we win) or hits the unique-index conflict (server short-circuits to the cached result). What's NOT retried: 4xx (request was bad), 5xx other than the four above (likely permanent), 200/207 (server already processed), AbortError (caller cancelled). Wired into the canary tool: `SummarizePdfTool`. Other 8 AI tools follow the same fetch-then-status-branch shape and are mechanical 1-line refactors deferred to a follow-up sweep. 22-assertion unit suite (`scripts/test-fetch-ai-retry.mjs`) covers every retry branch: 200 first try, 503в†’200, 503в†’502в†’200, 503Г—3, 400, 500, TypeError + recover, TypeError exhaust, 408 retry, bodyFactory called per-attempt. Total: 3166 passed, 0 failed across 37 suites (was 3144/36). M-series count now **16 of 25 shipped + 1 verified-canonical (M8)**.

- [x] **M9 part 2 вЂ” extend handoff to non-PageEditor runners + extract shared infrastructure.** Commit `3b01835` (2026-04-29). - [x] **Task #192: DOM virtualization for huge thumbnail grids.** Commit `77e655c` (2026-04-28). New `components/tools/useVirtualGrid.ts` hook computes visible rows from `window.scrollY + viewport height + container's document-relative top`. Below the threshold (80 items) the hook returns "render all", so small grids stay simple. Above the threshold, only the visible window + 2-row overscan is rendered, and the outer wrapper holds `totalHeight` so scroll geometry matches a fully-rendered grid. Why window-scroll instead of a custom scroll container: the tool pages are single-flow vertical layouts where the BODY scrolls вЂ” wrapping the grid in its own scroll container would break reading flow and add a nested scrollbar. ResizeObserver tracks container width; `getBoundingClientRect` on every (passive) scroll tick tracks document-relative top вЂ” accurate enough for 60fps with no IntersectionObserver tree. Sizing mirrors CSS auto-fill math: `cols = floor((containerWidth + gap) / (minColWidth + gap))`, `colW = (containerWidth - (cols - 1) * gap) / cols`, `rowH = colW Г— itemAspectRatio + itemFooterHeight + gap`. Wired into `PageGridTool` (used by Extract / Delete pages and any future thumbnail-selection variant). Uses the FIRST thumbnail's aspect ratio for row-height вЂ” pixel-perfect for single-orientation docs (the common case); landscape pages center-align in their tile envelope on mixed-orientation docs. `PdfSortPagesTool` intentionally untouched вЂ” its drag-to-reorder UX needs all items mounted at once. Verified: tsc clean; 2811/0 across 32 suites; all 6 affected routes (Extract/Delete/Stamp/PageNumbers/FreeDraw/ImageWatermark) return 200 post-deploy; `/api/health` reports `commit:"77e655ccd998"`. **Mid-deploy Task #20 cascade:** workers hit `pthread_create: Resource temporarily unavailable` after multiple SSH-pkicks during the auto-pull jam вЂ” Hostinger plan-level thread cap is shared across the account, and pkick + LSAPI auto-respawn together exceeded the cap. Site recovered after thread-pool reaped the failed-thread state. Lesson: ONE pkick max per deploy cycle, then wait for hPanel "Stop running process" if more is needed.

- [x] **Task #191: UI copy style guide + canonical error strings sweep.** Commit `79f1400` (2026-04-28). New `docs/UI_COPY.md` captures voice for buttons, errors, dropzone prompts, helper text, busy states, and success messages. Three rules: direct (no please), imperative on actions, specific over polite. Includes a canonical-errors table so future tools can copy verbatim instead of inventing variants. Sweep applies the canonical "non-PDF dropped" and "no file attached" errors across 35 tool components вЂ” replacing 8 different inconsistent phrasings (`"Please drop a PDF file."`, `"Attach a PDF first."`, `"Attach a PDF to fill & sign."`, `"Attach a PDF to rewrite."`, `"Attach a PDF to redact."`, `"Attach a PDF to TL;DR."`, `"Attach a PDF to summarize."`, `"Attach a PDF to translate."`, `"Attach a PDF to extract tables from."`) with two canonical lines (`"That's not a PDF. Drop a .pdf file to continue."` and `"Drop a PDF first."`). Verified: tsc clean; 2811/0 across 32 suites; zero remaining `"Please drop"` / `"Attach a PDF"` strings in `components/tools/`.

- [x] **Task #190: Free Draw stroke move with hit-testing.** Commit `4251782` (2026-04-28). Adds a Draw/Move mode toggle to the Free Draw tool. In Move mode, pointerdown does point-to-segment-distance hit-testing against existing strokes (within `strokeWidth/2 + 6px` slack) and grab-and-drag translates the matched stroke by absolute delta from the original click. Walks strokes in REVERSE order so the visually-topmost stroke wins on overlap (matches z-order). Selected stroke gets a soft blue halo (4px wider semi-transparent path behind it via `<g>` group) so users see what they grabbed. Hit-test math: standard projection onto each (P_i, P_{i+1}) segment with the parameter clamp to [0, 1], then Euclidean distance to the projected point. Tolerance scales with stroke width вЂ” thin strokes get a tight target, fat strokes are easier to grab. Snapshots `origPoints` at pointerdown so all moves are absolute deltas off the original (incremental drift would compound rounding errors). Clamps delta against page bounds so no point goes off-page. Cursor signals mode: `crosshair` while drawing, `grab` in move mode, `grabbing` while dragging. Empty-canvas hint in move mode tells users to switch to Draw first if no strokes exist yet. Mode persists across page navigation alongside color + width (`resetPageContent` only clears strokes). Verified: tsc clean; 2811/0 across 32 suites; `/tool/free-draw-pdf` returns 200; `/api/health` reports `commit:"42517827cf51"`.

- [x] **Task #189: Stamp + Page Numbers live page-1 preview.** Commit `6df9ab6` (2026-04-28, with nudge `f12dac8`). Both runners get a WYSIWYG preview of page 1 with the watermark / page number rendered as a CSS overlay at the configured position, opacity, color, font size, and rotation. Users iterate on settings and see the result instantly without having to apply + download + check + redo. New shared hook `components/tools/useFirstPagePreview.ts` renders page 1 once via PDFium (the existing `rasterize-page` op) and exposes pt+px dimensions; the hook revokes prior object URLs on file change and unmount. Each tool overlays its specific element using container-query units (`cqh`) so the on-screen glyph size scales with the preview's responsive width. Position math mirrors the corresponding op exactly: Stamp gets diagonal-rotated-45В° / center / top / bottom presets; Page Numbers gets 6 corner positions Г— 4 format styles. Helper "Stamps on all N pages" / "Numbers all N pages" pill in the top-right corner of the preview tells multi-page docs what's coming. Why not PageEditorTool: these are global configs, not click-to-place editors вЂ” the preview is informational, not interactive. Verified: tsc clean; 2811/0 across 32 suites; both `/tool/stamp-pdf` and `/tool/page-numbers` return 200.

- [x] **Task #188: Image Watermark v2 вЂ” visual click-to-place.** Commit `42058b1` (2026-04-28, with nudge `a60c681`). The op gains an optional `customPositionPt` (PDF points, bottom-left origin) вЂ” when provided, overrides the preset; per-page clamping keeps the image on-page even on mixed-orientation docs. Coordinate model: editor onClick converts CSS coords в†’ rendered px в†’ PDF points via `renderScale`, then anchors the click at the watermark's CENTER (intuitive "place it here" UX) by offsetting bottom-left by half-width / half-height. Live ghost outline switches between dashed-blue (custom click) and dashed-gray (preset). - [x] **Task #187: Resize handles on Highlight + Redact rects.** Commit `1e846b7` (2026-04-28). Mirrors the #181 Add Hyperlinks pattern across the other two rect-editing tools: each saved rect now renders 4 corner handles (NW/NE/SW/SE, 24Г—24 hit area, 10Г—10 visible indicator). Pointer-down on a handle snapshots the ORIGINAL rect (`origRect`) so all subsequent moves are absolute deltas вЂ” incremental drift was a real bug when clamping to page bounds during the initial Add Hyperlinks build. `applyResize` is corner-aware: dragging NW shrinks from x/y; dragging SE shrinks from w/h; minimum 8Г—8 keeps the rect interactable; final clamp to page bounds prevents off-page overflow. Resize handlers live alongside the #186 move handlers вЂ” pointer-down on a handle takes priority over the rect body's drag handler via `stopPropagation`, and `setPointerCapture` keeps events flowing even when the cursor leaves the handle. Helper text updated to "draw rectangles to mark, click X to remove, drag to reposition, corners to resize." Highlight and Redact now have full create/move/resize/delete parity with Add Hyperlinks. - [x] **Task #186: Drag-to-reposition Highlight + Redact rects.** Commit `59ec45f` (2026-04-28, with `86023ae` empty-commit nudge after auto-pull jam). Mirrors #180 from Add Hyperlinks. After placing a rect, users had to delete and redraw if they wanted it 20px to the left вЂ” now they can grab the rect body and drag it. `movingRef` (useRef) holds `{index, originX, originY, origRect}` snapshot at pointer-down so all moves are absolute deltas off the original position; `setPointerCapture` on the rect element keeps the pointer-move stream flowing even after the cursor exits the rect bounds. `applyMove` clamps to page width/height so users can't drag a rect off-page. - [x] **Task #175: Per-stroke delete on Free Draw.** Commit `b47e971` (2026-04-28). Free Draw was the last visual editor without per-element delete вЂ” only Undo (last stroke) and Clear All. Per-stroke delete via canvas hit-testing would be ambiguous on overlapping strokes (a click at coordinate X might land on 2-3 strokes), so a list-panel approach in the config sidesteps that and matches the saved-links pattern Add Hyperlinks already uses. The list shows for each stroke: a 16Г—16 color swatch, "Stroke N" header, point count + width subline, and an X delete button. Scrollable (max 168px). .map iterates state.strokes (not realStrokes-filtered) so visible-index for delete matches state-index splice target вЂ” sub-2-point in-flight strokes render as null inside the map. Brings Free Draw to parity with Add Hyperlinks (per-link list), Highlight (per-rect chip), and Redact (per-rect chip). **Deploy diagnostic finding (Task #20-adjacent):** auto-pull DID complete at 10:56 (build folder advanced to 44a2c97, `.next` artifacts re-emitted) but the running Next.js worker held onto its old code вЂ” `/api/health` continued to report `cc991b7` while the build folder was at `44a2c97`. Empty-commit nudge didn't help because the build was never the problem. Fix: SSH `pkill -9 -u u692382124 -f "next-server\|server.js"` per CLAUDE.md В§5 вЂ” runtime respawned in seconds, picked up the new build, `/api/health` flipped to `commit:"44a2c97a4ee8"`. **Lesson for future sessions:** if `last-source` is at HEAD but `/api/health` reports an older SHA, it's a stale-worker problem, not an auto-pull jam вЂ” go straight to the SSH worker kick instead of empty-commit nudges. 5 visual-editor routes verified 200 post-deploy.

Chip is hidden during mid-drag on the LAST rect (would self-delete during drag), while busy=true (apply in flight), and for tiny stray-click rects (w<8 or h<8). pointerdown stopPropagation prevents the chip click from firing the overlay's "start a new rect" handler. - [x] **Task #173: Stream thumbnails progressively into the UI.** Commit `81664e2` (2026-04-28). Yesterday's #172 hook extraction set up the plumbing; this turns it on. For a 500-page PDF, users used to stare at a spinner for 30-50 seconds before seeing any thumbnails вЂ” now they see thumbnails appearing live as the rasterizer works through pages (page 1 lands at ~80ms, page 2 at ~160ms, etc). `lib/pdf/ops/rasterize.ts` gains an optional `onPage(page: RasterPage)` callback that fires per-page BEFORE `onProgress` (so subscribers can mutate UI state in the same paint frame); returning a Promise pauses the loop for back-pressure. `usePdfThumbnails.render()` switches from awaiting the full batch + map-to-thumbnails-at-end to pushing each thumbnail to state inside `onPage` as it arrives вЂ” internal `collected[]` buffer mutated in place; `setThumbnails([...collected])` spreads to a fresh array so React detects the change. The resolved return value still gives consumers the full array (Sort relies on this for the `.map((t,i) => ...sourceIndex)` enrich). PageGridTool / PdfSplitTool relaxed grid-render gating from `stage === "ready" && thumbnails.length > 0` в†’ `thumbnails.length > 0 && stage !== "applying"`, so the grid appears as soon as page 1 lands; the rendering progress bar stays mounted above it until done. Apply button stays gated on `stage === "ready"` so users can't apply mid-stream. Sort intentionally untouched вЂ” its drag-to-reorder UX requires all pages loaded before interaction. - [x] **Task #172: Extract `usePdfThumbnails` hook.** Commit `8b3517c` (2026-04-28). PageGridTool, PdfSortPagesTool, and PdfSplitTool each had a near-identical 25-line block (rasterizePdf import + map results to {pageNumber, thumbnailUrl, width, height} + revoke object URLs on unmount). Three copies meant three places to keep in sync, and made it hostile to land virtualization for huge-PDF thumbnail tools cleanly. Extracted to `components/tools/usePdfThumbnails.ts` вЂ” hook owns thumbnails state, blob в†’ object URL conversion, URL.createObjectURL/revokeObjectURL lifecycle, progress + rendering + error state. Returns `{thumbnails, rendering, progress, error, render(bytes), reset()}`. Default options: `scale=0.5`, `quality=0.7`. Unmount cleanup uses a ref so the revoke doesn't refire on every thumbnails change. PageGridTool and PdfSplitTool use hook's thumbnails directly; PdfSortPagesTool enriches with `sourceIndex` (it tracks original positions for the reorder op). PdfMergeTool intentionally untouched (different shape: one page from each of many files). PageEditorTool also untouched (uses single-page on-demand `rasterize-page.ts`). Net: -118/+179 LOC across 4 files (hook is +130 LOC of which ~40 is comments/docstring, the 3 consumers shed -75 LOC of duplication). - [x] **Task #171: Per-page state persistence + multi-page apply.** Commit `bd47500` (2026-04-28). Yesterday's #170 added page navigation but reset state on every jump, so users could only ever apply edits to one page per file load вЂ” sharp edge a user hits within seconds of trying it on a real PDF. Today's ship makes state persist across pages and lets apply walk every edited page in a single pass, chaining bytes through the per-page op. `PageEditorTool` props are now a discriminated union вЂ” `multiPage: true` switches the apply signature to receive `PageEditEntry<TState>[]` (each entry carries pageIndex + state + dims snapshot for pxв†’pt conversion across mixed-orientation pages); single-page mode unchanged for Crop and Add Text Box. New `hasEdits(state)` predicate decides which pages roll into the entries array; new `resetPageContent(state)` predicate preserves global config (color, opacity, image, pen width, scale) when navigating to a fresh page so the user's tool config sticks across navigation. Runner shows a "N other pages edited" pill in the navigator when stashed edits exist. 5 visual editors (Highlight / Redact / Add Hyperlinks / Sign / Free Draw) opted in; each apply now iterates entries and chains bytes through one op call per page. ### Free tools (client-side WASM)

- [x] **`/tool/page-numbers` runner live.** New `PageNumbersTool` component ships two modes in one runner: (a) **Page numbers** вЂ” 4 formats (`1`, `1 / N`, `Page 1`, `Page 1 of N`) Г— 6 positions (TL/TC/TR/BL/BC/BR), adjustable font size 8вЂ“24pt; (b) **Watermark** вЂ” user-entered text (в‰¤40 chars) drawn diagonally at 45В° across page center, adjustable font size 24вЂ“96pt, adjustable opacity 5вЂ“60%. Built on `pdf-lib` with `StandardFonts.Helvetica` / `HelveticaBold`; fully client-side, no server round-trip. Wired into `LIVE_TOOL_IDS` in `app/tool/[id]/page.tsx`. Flips T5 in TEST_PLAN.md from Pending в†’ Ready-to-test. (2026-04-20)
- [x] **`/tool/to-pdf` runner live.** New `ImageToPdfTool` component accepts JPG + PNG (в‰¤20 MB each), embeds each image as a page, and saves one PDF. Supports three layout modes: fit-to-image (each page sized to source dimensions, capped at 3000pt), US Letter with centered fit, A4 with centered fit. Adjustable page margin (0вЂ“72pt) in Letter/A4 modes. Multi-file reorder + remove controls mirror MergePdfTool. Built on `pdf-lib` `embedJpg` / `embedPng`. Brings the live free-tool count to six. (2026-04-20)
- [x] **`/tool/protect` runner live.** New `ProtectPdfTool` component ships two modes in one runner: (a) **Protect** вЂ” set user password (в‰Ґ 4 chars, confirm-field enforced), optional separate owner password, per-permission grid (allow printing / copying text / editing / annotations); (b) **Unlock** вЂ” provide current password, strip the encryption on save so the output PDF is decrypted. Auto-detects whether the dropped file is already encrypted and flips the default mode. Built on `@cantoo/pdf-lib`, a maintained pdf-lib fork that adds the PDF encryption handler (pdf-lib 1.17 can read but not write encrypted PDFs). `@cantoo/pdf-lib` is dynamic-imported only on this runner вЂ” the other free-tool bundles are unaffected. Fully client-side вЂ” the password never leaves the browser; same "Stays in your browser" reassurance card as the other free tools. Also fixed a Next 14 prerender break: added a `<Suspense>` boundary around `<LoginForm>` in `app/login/page.tsx` because `useSearchParams()` (for the `?reset=1` flash added with the reset-redemption flow) requires one for static generation. Brings the live free-tool count to seven. (2026-04-20)
- [x] **`/tool/rotate` upgraded to true "Rotate & Reorder".** Previous runner only rotated. New `RotatePdfTool` is a single-screen flow with three operations: (a) bulk row вЂ” "Rotate all 90В° CW", "Rotate all 180В°", "Rotate all 90В° CCW", "Reverse order", "Undo all edits"; (b) per-page row вЂ” show page index + "was #N" badge when reordered + accumulated rotation chip + в†‘ / в†“ / rotate-CW / rotate-CCW / delete buttons; (c) Apply & download builds the output via `copyPages` in the edited order, applying each page's accumulated rotation. Output filename suffix is chosen per edit kind (`-rotated`, `-reordered`, `-edited`). Edits stored as a delta from source so "Undo all edits" reloads the file cleanly. Lives up to the registry's "Rotate & Reorder" / "Fix orientation and rearrange pages" promise. (2026-04-20)

### API / monitoring

- [x] **`/api/health` endpoint shipped.** Pings the DB with `SELECT 1`, returns `{ ok, service, commit, uptimeSec, db: { ok, latencyMs|error }, ts }`. Status code 200 on healthy / 503 on DB failure. `cache-control: no-store` so Cloudflare never serves a stale probe. Consumed by the status page and safe to bind as the Cloudflare origin health check. Error strings sanitized вЂ” never echoes DSN fragments. **Verified live 2026-04-20 01:50 UTC: `{ "ok": true, "db": { "ok": true, "latencyMs": 48 }}`.** (2026-04-20)

- [x] **`/api/payments/probe` GET endpoint shipped.** Public, read-only diagnostic route at `app/api/payments/probe/route.ts` (141 lines). Returns the provider registry's current state: `{ ok: true, configuredIds: string[], providers: [{ id, displayName, capabilities: {oneTime, subscriptions, refunds, partialRefunds, webhooks}, supportedCurrencies: string[] }], ts }`. Mirrors `/api/health` conventions: `runtime = "nodejs"`, `dynamic = "force-dynamic"`, `cache-control: no-store, no-cache, must-revalidate`, `x-probe-service: payments` response header, ISO timestamp in body. Three response paths: (a) no provider configured в†’ 200 with `{ ok: true, configuredIds: [], providers: [] }` (sandbox-safe вЂ” app is healthy, it just has no processor wired yet; does NOT 503); (b) adapters load clean в†’ 200 with populated `providers`; (c) adapter factory throws в†’ 503 with `{ ok: false, error: "adapter_load_failed" }` (`err.message` deliberately NOT echoed вЂ” adapter stack traces can include env-var names / config paths). Auth posture: public, matches `/api/health` precedent. The response body carries **no new recon signal** beyond what the edge CSP allowlist already reveals (adapter capabilities + currencies are inferable from the CSP directives in `.htaccess`; `id` + `displayName` are the only literal strings, both already public in the checkout UI button labels). **Why it exists**: after the 2026-04-21 `RAZORPAY_*` env-var deploy via hPanel, confirming the values reached the Next.js runtime required SSH + `tr "\0" "\n" < /proc/<pid>/environ` on the live worker PIDs вЂ” a fragile pattern that doesn't scale for post-deploy checks or monitoring hooks. With the probe live, `curl -s https://pdfcraftai.com/api/payments/probe | jq` answers "did the env vars propagate?" directly. Wirable into a Cloudflare origin health check the same way `/api/health` is вЂ” if `RAZORPAY_*` secrets get wiped by a bad redeploy, `configuredIds` flips from `["razorpay"]` to `[]` and monitoring can alert. Imports `listConfiguredProviders` + `listConfiguredProviderIds` from `lib/payments/registry.ts` вЂ” both already exported and stable. Companion `/api/payments/order` REST wrapper deferred вЂ” `createCheckoutAction` server action already covers the UI happy path, so the REST mirror is a lower-priority convenience and is out until a concrete non-UI caller emerges. Pushed as `7391a8a feat(payments): add /api/payments/probe diagnostic endpoint`; Hostinger auto-deploy landed at ~135 s (`/api/health` `commit` flipped `b525d8475cee` в†’ `7391a8a56d89`). Live prod verification at 2026-04-21T05:37:06Z: `curl -si https://pdfcraftai.com/api/payments/probe` в†’ HTTP/2 200 with `x-probe-service: payments`, `cache-control: no-store, no-cache, must-revalidate`, `cf-cache-status: DYNAMIC` (Cloudflare respecting bypass); body = `{"ok":true,"configuredIds":["razorpay"],"providers":[{"id":"razorpay","displayName":"Razorpay","capabilities":{"oneTime":true,"subscriptions":true,"refunds":true,"partialRefunds":true,"webhooks":true},"supportedCurrencies":["INR","USD"]},...}`. **This is also now the cleanest in-prod proof for Tasks #7 + #8**: `configuredIds: ["razorpay"]` can only ever come back from the registry if all three `RAZORPAY_*` env vars survived the hPanel deploy AND the Razorpay adapter factory loaded without throwing вЂ” stronger evidence than the earlier `tr "\0" "\n" < /proc/<pid>/environ` SSH-environ trick. (2026-04-21)

- [x] **`lib/payments/router.ts` shipped вЂ” geo-aware checkout router** (commit `2e28c68`). Turned the illustrative `routeCheckout` snippet in `GEO_LAUNCH_POLICY.md` В§3.2 into a real typed module with a pure decision function `routeCheckoutByCountry(country)` that returns a discriminated `RouteDecision` union: (a) `action: "route"` with `rail: "razorpay"/"paddle"` + `currency: "INR"/"USD"` for Tier 1 (28 countries вЂ” IN goes to Razorpay INR; all others to Paddle USD); (b) `action: "defer"` + `status: 403` + `reason: "tier2_deferred"` for Tier 2 (EU27 + CH/NO/IS/LI + CN/RU/BY = 34 countries); (c) `action: "block"` + `status: 451` + `reason: "tier3_sanctioned"` for Tier 3 (IR/SY/KP/CU вЂ” defense-in-depth; the Cloudflare WAF rule blocks these at the edge with 403 on free plan before origin sees them); (d) `action: "unknown"` + `status: 403` + `reason: "geo_unknown"` for missing/XX/T1/empty headers so the UI can prompt for manual country selection instead of silently defaulting. Case-insensitive + whitespace-tolerant (`trim + toUpperCase`). Subdivision codes (UA-43/40/14/09/65/23) intentionally NOT in `TIER_3_COUNTRIES` вЂ” those are edge-only per the WAF rule. Catchall (country not in any tier) routes to Paddle USD per policy В§3.2 guidance that Paddle's own KYC geo-refuses anything we can't process. Also exports `readCountryHeader(headers)` as a Next.js-friendly `CF-IPCountry` extractor (accepts both `Headers` instance + plain record). Pure function вЂ” no DB, no network, no logging side-effects; callers at higher layers own the 2-year audit-trail log write per GEO_LAUNCH_POLICY В§5. **Crucially, does NOT modify `lib/payments/checkout-actions.ts`** вЂ” the live Razorpay IN checkout codepath is untouched. Integration follows when Paddle adapter keys land (Task #1 blocker) because wiring `routeCheckoutByCountry` into `createCheckoutAction` only becomes behavior-correct once Paddle is actually available to catch the non-IN Tier 1 traffic. - [x] **Tier-2 deferred-region email waitlist shipped вЂ” Task #3 sub-item (3)** (commit `d0f00d4`). Additive frontend + DB machinery so visitors from Tier-2 countries (`routeCheckoutByCountry(country) в†’ action: "defer"`) can opt in to a launch-announcement email instead of bouncing. Independent of Paddle; unblocks further shippable work before MoR keys arrive. Five files in one commit: (1) `db/schema/app.ts` adds `geoWaitlist` Drizzle table вЂ” `id` UUID PK, `email` (varchar 320, lowercased on insert), `country` (ISO-2, server-side validated against `TIER_2_COUNTRIES`), `reason` enum (`tier2_deferred` for checkout-turnaway vs. `tier2_notify` for proactive marketing-surface opt-in), `source` (free-form UI origin like `checkout_defer` / `pricing_country_picker` / `marketing_footer` for funnel analytics), `consent_text` (stores the EXACT sentence the user clicked вЂ” GDPR audit trail, text column so copy length stays unbounded), `user_agent` (varchar 512), `ip_hash` (SHA-256(ip + server salt), 64-char hex; raw IP never persisted), `created_at`, `notified_at` (set when the launch job actually emails them вЂ” prevents double-send). `UNIQUE(email, country)` index lets one address track multiple countries while blocking literal dupes; `INDEX(country)` optimizes the launch-job country cut; `INDEX(created_at)` for admin "signups this week" dashboards. (2) `db/migrations/0004_geo_waitlist.sql` hand-authored DDL matching the pattern in 0002/0003 вЂ” `CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS` + 2 post-create `CREATE INDEX` statements (idempotent, safe to re-run against a prod schema that already has the table). (3) `app/api/geo/waitlist/route.ts` POST handler вЂ” Zod validation chain including `z.literal(true)` on `consent` (can't be `false` or missing) + a refine that rejects anything not in `TIER_2_COUNTRIES` with `"country_not_eligible"` (Tier 1 IN/US/etc. shouldn't see the form; Tier 3 IR/SY/KP/CU can't be onboarded under sanctions; unknown в†’ we don't know what country to promise), in-memory 60s rate limit keyed by both email AND IP (email checked first вЂ” cheaper reject path), IP hashing with server-side `GEO_WAITLIST_IP_SALT` env var (fallback to per-process `randomUUID` so session-level dedupe survives a missing env without crashing), `cf-connecting-ip` preferred over `x-forwarded-for` for the IP source, ER_DUP_ENTRY (errno 1062) caught on insert and returned as soft 200 with `alreadyListed: true` so the UI doesn't expose whether the address is new or known. Console log is country + source only вЂ” no raw email in production logs. (4) `components/geo/DeferredRegionNotify.tsx` `"use client"` React component taking `{country, source?, reason?, countryName?}` props. Email input + consent checkbox (NOT pre-checked, GDPR) + submit button. Submit stays disabled until consent is true (defense-in-depth; server still re-validates). The consent sentence template (`"I agree to receive a one-time email from pdfcraftai.com when the service launches in ${countryName || country}. I understand I can withdraw consent at any time by emailing support@pdfcraftai.com."`) is built via `useMemo`, shown next to the checkbox, and POSTed verbatim in `consentText` вЂ” stored row-for-row so copy changes over time are auditable. Error-code mapping translates the server's short codes (`rate_limited_email`, `country_not_eligible`, `consent_required`, `Invalid email`) to user-visible copy client-side so no translation table needs shipping with the API. Styling reuses the existing `ContactForm` visual language вЂ” no new design tokens.
